11a1(myang 'das): rnamang bzhi ste/ gang zhig gis nan tan byas na/ tshangs pa chen po'i gan su skye bar 'gyur ro// rigs kyi ru ltar na/ chad med pa rnams la bregs

316b8(myang 'das): gyur pa spong bar gyur cig/ mu gi byung ba'i dusu chog 'das par gyur cig/ nang dang gor byung ba'i dusu span pa'i rgyal po ro gyur te/ nad kyi rgyan smar dang / nor rang rin po
317a1(myang 'das): ji za shes pa yang bzhin du sbyin par gyur pa nang rnams bsal bar gyur cig/ mtshon gyi bskal pa'i cha mthu stobs chen po yong bar gyur pa gang ba
317a2(myang 'das): 'cha bar lus par chod par gyur cig/ sems can gyi 'jigs pa rnam pa sna tshogs gcong bar gyur pa ni 'di lta ste/ 'chi ba'i 'chang ba 'am/ brdeg pa 'am chu'ang pa 'am/ 
317a3(myang 'das): rgyal po 'am/ rkun bro 'am dngul ba 'am/ khrims 'jig pa 'am/ mi snyan pa 'am/ ngan song ngam/ de lta bu la sogs pa'i 'jigs pa kun yongasu gcod par gyur cig/ pha dang bang
317a4(myang 'das): mkhan po dag bla ma la shin tu bkur bsti byeng par gyu dacig mkhan po dang sdang ba la byams pa cher ba'i sebs skye bar gyur cig/ rtag tu dran pa
317a5(myang 'das): bar gzhag phywa dang / stong pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rnam grang sa dang / rten cing 'brel te byung ba bcu gnyis dang / skye ring 'gog pa la sogs pa'i lhag mthong dang
317a6(myang 'das): dbugs phyi nang bgrang ba dang / lnga'i spyod pa dang tshangs pa'i spyod pa dang / 'phags pa'i spyod pa dang / rdo rje lta bu'i ting 'dzin dang dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting 'dzin la sogs
317a7(myang 'das): ba bsgom par gyur cig/ dkon mchog gsum med pa'i gnasu bdag nyid kyis rab tu zhi ba'i sems thob cing gal te/ lus dang sems nyon mongs pa chen po myong
317a8(myang 'das): ngan yang bla na meng pa'i byang chub kyi sems stong bar ma gyur cig/ nyan thos dang ra sangs rgyas kyi sems kyis tshag pa 'dzin cing // dkon mtshag gsum med pa'i sa
317b1(myang 'das): su rtag tu mu stegs can gyi chos la rab tu byung ste/ ngan par lta ba 'jig cing de'i chos la goms par mi byed par chos kyi dbang dang / sems kyi dbang thob par gyur
317b2(myang 'das): cig 'dus byas kyi chos kyi skyon gsal bar mthong bar gyur cig ji ltar srog phangs pa lus skyong ba la 'jigs pa ltar bdag kyang theg pa gnyis kyi lam gyi 'dras
317b3(myang 'das): lu la 'jigs par cig/ ji ltar sems can rnamasu bcu rtsa gsum gnas kyi bde ba la bos pa ltar/ sems can gyi phyir 'an song gsum la nges par gyur cig
317b4(myang 'das): sngams can gcig gi phyir yang bskal pa tshang mang ba 'i bar du sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal myong yang 'gyod pa'i sems mi skye bar gyur cig/ gan
317b5(myang 'das): gyi rnyeng par thong na/ phra dog mi sbed cing ji ltar bdag bde ba rdzob pa ltar rtag tu dga' brgya cig/ gal te dkon mchog gsum da drang na na bza' dang
317b6(myang 'das): bshos dang / gzims cha dang / gnas khang dang sman gyi rkyen sman dang / mar me dang me tog dang spos dang / rol mo dang gdugs rang ba ngan dang rin po che sA bcu
317b7(myang 'das): gyis yongasu mchod par gyur cig/ gal te sangs rgyas kyi tshul khribs pados na shin tu brtan par bsrungs te/ nams kyang 'jig rten pa'i mtshan cing ma bskyed
317b8(myang 'das): cig gal te byang chub sems dpa'i dka' ba spyang pa thob na rab tu dga' mes te/ 'gyod pa'i sems pa bskyad cig/ bdag gi sngon gyi gnas kyi dngos po dra ni
